debug_decisions = {
	TUR_reload_minority_values = {
		allowed = { original_tag = TUR }
		complete_effect = { ottoman_minority_variable_check = yes }
		ai_will_do = { base = 0 }
	}
	TUR_update_party_popularities = {
		allowed = { original_tag = TUR }
		complete_effect = {
			TUR_government_stability_calculate = yes
			TUR_government_popularity_calculate = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = { base = 0 }
	}
	TUR_bop_right = {
		allowed = { original_tag = TUR }
		complete_effect = {
			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = TUR_government_committee_struggle
				value = 2
			}
			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = TUR_local_central_rule
				value = 2
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = { base = 0 }
	}
	TUR_bop_left = {
		allowed = { original_tag = TUR }
		complete_effect = {
			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = TUR_government_committee_struggle
				value = -2
			}
			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = TUR_local_central_rule
				value = -2
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = { base = 0 }
	}
}

GER_great_war = {
	TUR_surrender_to_entente = {
		allowed = { tag = TUR }
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_support
		fire_only_once = yes
		activation = {
			check_variable = { TUR_government_stability_var < 26 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_specific_crisis_on_hand }
			has_capitulated = no
			is_in_faction = yes
			is_faction_leader = no
			is_subject = no
			has_war_with = FRA
			FRA = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				is_subject = no
				NOT = { has_country_flag = great_war_loser }
			}
			has_global_flag = great_war
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = great_war_loser
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
				has_global_flag = GER_capitulation
				has_global_flag = FRA_capitulation
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					surrender_progress > 0.4
					# war is losing
					OR = {
						any_neighbor_country = {
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							has_capitulated = yes
						}
						faction_leader = { surrender_progress > 0.1 }
					}
				}
				# so fucked
				AND = {
					has_war_support < 0.2
					has_stability < 0.2
				}
				# Constantinople lost
				NOT = { controls_state = 347 }
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_yakub_cemils_coup_succeess }
					has_country_flag = TUR_yakub_cemils_coup_succeess
				}
			}
		}
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = TUR_government_stability_higher_than_25
				check_variable = { TUR_government_stability_var > 25 }
			}
			controls_state = 347
			surrender_progress < 0.4
			has_war_support > 0.2
			has_stability > 0.2
			NOT = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_yakub_cemils_coup_succeess }
					has_country_flag = TUR_yakub_cemils_coup_succeess
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_capitulated = yes
				has_war = no
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
				has_global_flag = GER_capitulation
				has_global_flag = FRA_capitulation
			}
		}
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = no
		days_mission_timeout = 30
		timeout_effect = {
			add_ideas = TUR_mudros_armistice
			if = {
				limit = { has_war_with = ENG }
				ENG = { country_event = { id = ww1_england.264 hours = 3 } }
			}
			else = { FRA = { country_event = { id = ww1_england.264 hours = 3 } } }
			hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = ww1_england.265 hours = 10 } }
		}
	}
	TUR_declare_jihad = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_nationalism
		allowed = { tag = TUR }
		available = {
			any_enemy_country = {
				is_major = yes
				is_in_faction = yes
			}
			has_global_flag = great_war
		}
		visible = { NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_abolished_caliph } }
		cost = 25
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			add_war_support = 0.05
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					controller = {
						OR = {
							original_tag = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = TUR
							is_subject_of = TUR
						}
					}
					OR = {
						is_arabian_core = yes
						is_core_of = PER
						is_core_of = ALB
						is_core_of = EGY
					}	
					has_resistance = yes
				}
				add_compliance = 3
			}
			every_enemy_country = {
				every_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						has_resistance = yes
						OR = {
							is_arabian_core = yes
							is_core_of = PER
							is_core_of = ALB
							is_core_of = EGY
						}
					}
					add_resistance = 15
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = TUR_jihad_declared
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_declare_jihad_tt
			add_to_variable = { TUR_aoabe_army_morale_factor = 0.02 }
			set_variable = { TUR_aoabe_weekly_casualties_war_support = 0.002 }
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 1000
		}
	}

					type = destroyer
					count = 2
				}

						type = dockyard

						damage = 1

			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_naval_vessels_receive_damage
			damage_units = {
				province = 3686
				str_damage = 0.3
				ratio = yes
				army = no
				navy = yes
			}
			damage_units = {
				province = 11670
				str_damage = 0.3
				ratio = yes
				army = no
				navy = yes
			}
			damage_units = {

				navy = yes
			}
			damage_units = {
				province = 9884
				str_damage = 0.3
				ratio = yes
				army = no
				navy = yes
			}
			set_country_flag = TUR_black_sea_raid_happened
		}

	TUR_invoke_senussiya_alliance = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_nationalism
		allowed = {
			original_tag = TUR
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = great_war
			is_subject = no
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
			}
			FROM = {
				is_subject = no
				is_in_faction = no
				OR = {
					has_government = neutrality
					has_government = fascism
				}	
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = TUR
					has_war_together_with = TUR
					has_country_flag = LBA_modus_vivendi_of_acroma
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					LBA = {
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				is_in_faction = yes
			}	
		}
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				tag = LBA
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_war = yes
			any_country = {
				has_war_with = TUR
				any_owned_state = {
					is_core_of = LBA
				}
			}
		}
		days_remove = 14
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					LBA = {
						is_ai = yes				
					}
				}				
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = TUR
						any_owned_state = {
							is_core_of = LBA
						}
					}
					LBA = {
						add_to_war = {
							targeted_alliance = TUR
							enemy = PREV
						}	
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction = yes	
					}
					add_to_faction = LBA
				}
				else = {
					LBA = {
						country_event = generic.5
					}
				}
			}	
			LBA = {
				set_country_flag = TUR_invoke_senussiya_alliance
			}	
		}
		cost = 15
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				has_war_with = ITA
				factor = 1000
			}
			modifier = {
				date < 1915.11.1
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = TUR_combat_armenian_separatists
				has_completed_focus = TUR_exile_armenian_separatists
			}
			controls_state = FROM
			FROM = {

				OR = {

					check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_enemy_local_supplies_armenian > 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		cost = 15
		days_remove = 30
		available = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_autonomous_vilayet }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_semi_autonomous_vilayet }
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			FROM = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_clash_against_armenian_gangs_tt
				add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_attrition = 0.1 }
			}
			ottoman_minority_variable_check = yes
		}
		remove_effect = {
			FROM = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_clash_against_armenian_gangs_tt2
				add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_attrition_armenian = -0.1 }
				add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_army_defence_factor_armenian = 0.05 }
				add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_enemy_local_supplies_armenian = -0.05 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { state = 347 } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_konstantiniyye_centralization_1
				add_to_variable = { global.TUR_konstantiniyye_centralization = 0.01 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						OR = {
							state = 1019
							state = 1035
						}
					}

				add_to_variable = { global.TUR_edirne_centralization = 0.01 }
			}

	TUR_integrate_macedonia = {
		icon = GFX_decision_hol_draw_up_staff_plans
		allowed = { original_tag = TUR }
		cost = 15
		state_target = yes
		targets = {
			345
			731
			184
			788
			225
			759
			203
			106
		}
		on_map_mode = map_only
		fire_only_once = yes
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = TUR_law_on_churches
			controls_state = FROM
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_south_slavic_minority }
				}
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
		}
		available = {
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority } }
					custom_trigger_tooltip = {
						tooltip = TUR_integrate_macedonia_tt1
						check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_attrition_greek < 0.01 }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_south_slavic_minority } }
					custom_trigger_tooltip = {
						tooltip = TUR_integrate_macedonia_tt2
						check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_attrition_south_slavic < 0.01 }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 184
							state = 759
						}
					}
					compliance > 40
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 203
							state = 106
							state = 225
							state = 788
							state = 731
						}
					}
					compliance > 60
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = { FROM = { add_core_of = TUR } }
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

		allowed = { original_tag = TUR }
		custom_cost_text = command_power_more_than_10
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 9.99 }
		state_target = yes
		targets = { 975 }
		on_map_mode = map_only
		days_remove = 30
		fire_only_once = yes
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = ikarian_revolt
			controls_state = FROM
			FROM = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
				check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_resistance_target_greek > 0 }
			}
		}
		available = {
			divisions_in_state = {
				type = infantry
				size > 0
				state = FROM
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
            divisions_in_state = {
				type = infantry
				size < 1
				state = FROM
			}
        }
		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -10 }
			FROM = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_combat_rebels_in_ahikerya_tt
				add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_attrition_greek = 0.3 }
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			FROM = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_combat_rebels_in_ahikerya_tt2
				add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_attrition_greek = -0.3 }
				add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_resistance_target_greek = -0.1 }
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
            FROM = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_combat_rebels_in_ahikerya_tt3
				add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_attrition_greek = -0.2 }
			}
        }
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

peace_deals = {
	TUR_sue_for_peace_ITA = {
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_support
		allowed = { tag = TUR }
		target_trigger = { FROM = { tag = ITA } }
		available = {
			has_war_with = ITA
			OR = {
				is_in_faction = no
				ITA = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = kis_firstbalkan_war
					has_war_with = BUL
					has_war_with = SER
					has_war_with = GRE
					any_enemy_country = {
						is_major = yes
						NOT = { original_tag = ITA }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = italo_turkish_war
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = ITA_libyan_war_mission_timeout
				has_global_flag = italo_turkish_war_ends
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = great_war }
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = great_war_ends
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = FRA
						is_in_faction_with = GER
						has_war_with = FRA
						has_war_with = GER
					}
				}
			}
			owns_state = 448
			owns_state = 450
			owns_state = 661
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = { ITA = { country_event = { id = ww1_italianturkish.4 hours = 3 } } }
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				has_war_with = ITA
				OR = {
					casualties > 50000
					ITA = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 448
						has_full_control_of_state = 450
						has_full_control_of_state = 661
						has_full_control_of_state = 663
					}
					AND = {
						any_owned_state = {
							is_controlled_by = ITA
							OR = {
								region = 25
								region = 129
								region = 202
							}
						}
						OR = {
							ITA = { controls_state = 448 }
							ITA = { controls_state = 450 }
						}
					}
					surrender_progress > 0.10
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 500
				OR = {
					has_war_with = BUL
					has_war_with = SER
					has_war_with = GRE
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						ITA = {
							surrender_progress < 0.05
						}
						NOT = {
							controls_state = 448
							controls_state = 450
						}
					}
					surrender_progress > 0.05
				}
			}
		}
	}
	TUR_sue_for_peace_BLL = {

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 500
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_historical_focus_on = no
					AND = {
						date < 1914.1.12	##force surrender if it last forever
						NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_must_won_bw1 }
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
					}
				}
				OR = {
					#historical trigger
					AND = {
						date < 1913.5.24
						casualties < 350000
						OR = {
							surrender_progress < 0.2
							any_controlled_state = { is_on_continent = europe }
						}
					}
					#dont surrender if you are wining the balkan war
					#ahistorical cases
					SER = {
						OR = {
							is_subject_of = TUR
							has_capitulated = yes
							surrender_progress > 0.3
						}
					}
					BUL = {
						OR = {
							is_subject_of = TUR
							has_capitulated = yes
							surrender_progress > 0.3
						}
					}
					GRE = {
						OR = {
							is_subject_of = TUR
							has_capitulated = yes
							surrender_progress > 0.3
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

TUR_local_conscription = {
	TUR_local_conscription_in_state = {
		icon = GFX_manpower_icon
		allowed = { original_tag = TUR }
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_ArmXP_10
		custom_cost_trigger = { has_army_experience > 9.99 }
		state_target = yes
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				check_variable = { TUR_turkish_state_level > 0 }
				check_variable = { TUR_local_conscription_in_state_var < TUR_turkish_state_level }
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				is_core_of = ROOT
				NOT = {
					has_state_category = city
					has_state_category = large_city
					has_state_category = metropolis
					has_state_category = megalopolis
				}
			}
		}
		on_map_mode = map_only
		days_remove = 7
		days_re_enable = 28
		visible = { has_completed_focus = TUR_the_new_recruitment_law }
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { army_experience = -10 } }
		remove_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_local_conscription_in_state_manpower_var = FROM.state_population }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_local_conscription_in_state_manpower_var = 500 }
			add_manpower = TUR_local_conscription_in_state_manpower_var
			hidden_effect = {

		icon = oil
		allowed = { tag = TUR }
		available = {
			OR = {

				is_in_faction_with = ENG
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
			NOT = { has_war_with = ENG }
			NOT = { has_war_with = GER }
			676 = {
				controller = {
					tag = ROOT
					has_full_control_of_state = PREV
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_decision = TUR_tpc_operations_in_kirkuk
				has_decision = TUR_tpc_operations_in_baghdad
				has_decision = TUR_tpc_operations_in_basra
			}
		}
		highlight_states = { highlight_state_targets = { state = 676 } }
		on_map_mode = decision_view_only
		cost = 50
		fire_only_once = no
		days_remove = TUR_turkish_petroleum_company_decision_time?120
		visible = { has_completed_focus = TUR_form_the_turkish_petroleum_company }
		complete_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = { TUR_add_debt_1_ENG = yes }
				50 = { TUR_add_debt_1_GER = yes }
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			676 = {
				add_resource = {
					type = oil
					amount = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = TUR_tpc_operations_in_mosul value = 2 compare = not_equals }
					check_variable = { var = TUR_tpc_operations_in_mosul value = 5 compare = not_equals }
					check_variable = { var = TUR_tpc_operations_in_mosul value = 9 compare = less_than }
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_tpc_operations_in_mosul_tt
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { var = TUR_tpc_operations_in_mosul value = 2 compare = equals } }
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = TUR_tpc_operations_in_mosul
					bonus = 0.3
					uses = 1
					category = synth_resources
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { var = TUR_tpc_operations_in_mosul value = 5 compare = equals } }
				676 = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = infrastructure
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { var = TUR_tpc_operations_in_mosul value = 9 compare = equals } }
				676 = {
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { var = TUR_tpc_operations_in_mosul value = 1 compare = greater_than_or_equals } } }

	TUR_investments_from_FRA = {
		icon = GFX_decision_hol_attract_foreign_investors
		allowed = { always = no }
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = FRA
				var:FRA.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = { NOT = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = TUR } }
				FRA = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_rumelia_mission }
						NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_rumelia_mission }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_anatolia_mission }
						NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_anatolia_mission }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_syria_mission }
						NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_syria_mission }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_mesapotamia_mission }
						NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_mesapotamia_mission }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_trablusgarp_mission }
						NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_trablusgarp_mission }
					}
					else = { NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_rumelia_mission } }
				}
			}
		}
		visible = { FRA = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans } }
		on_map_mode = decision_view_only
		activation = { always = no }
		days_mission_timeout = 180
		highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { state = var:FRA.ottoman_investment_targeted_state } }
		available = { hidden_trigger = { always = no } }
		is_good = yes
		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { FRA = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_infrastructure } }
				var:FRA.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = infrastructure
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				TUR_add_debt_5_FRA = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FRA = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_consumer } }
				var:FRA.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				TUR_add_debt_8_FRA = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FRA = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_military
							has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_dockyard
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { FRA = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_military } }
					var:FRA.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = arms_factory
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { FRA = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_dockyard } }
					var:FRA.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = dockyard
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
				TUR_add_debt_10_FRA = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FRA = { has_idea = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
				FRA = { remove_ideas = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FRA = { has_idea = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
				FRA = { remove_ideas = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FRA = { has_idea = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
				FRA = { remove_ideas = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans }
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = { FRA = { has_idea = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
					FRA = { remove_ideas = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { FRA = { has_idea = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
					FRA = { remove_ideas = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { FRA = { has_idea = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
					FRA = { remove_ideas = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans }
				}
			}
		}
	}

		highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { state = var:ENG.ottoman_investment_targeted_state } }
		available = { hidden_trigger = { always = no } }
		is_good = yes
		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { ENG = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_inENGstructure } }
				var:ENG.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = inENGstructure
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				TUR_add_debt_5_ENG = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ENG = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_consumer } }
				var:ENG.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				TUR_add_debt_8_ENG = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ENG = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_military
							has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_dockyard
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { ENG = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_military } }
					var:ENG.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = arms_factory
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { ENG = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_dockyard } }
					var:ENG.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = dockyard
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
				TUR_add_debt_10_ENG = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ENG = { has_idea = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
				ENG = { remove_ideas = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ENG = { has_idea = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
				ENG = { remove_ideas = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ENG = { has_idea = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
				ENG = { remove_ideas = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans }
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = { ENG = { has_idea = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
					ENG = { remove_ideas = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { ENG = { has_idea = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
					ENG = { remove_ideas = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { ENG = { has_idea = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
					ENG = { remove_ideas = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	TUR_investments_from_GER = {
		icon = GFX_decision_hol_attract_foreign_investors
		allowed = { always = no }
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = GER
				var:GER.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = { NOT = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = TUR } }
				GER = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_rumelia_mission }
						NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_rumelia_mission }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_anatolia_mission }
						NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_anatolia_mission }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_syria_mission }
						NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_syria_mission }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_mesapotamia_mission }
						NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_mesapotamia_mission }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_trablusgarp_mission }
						NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_trablusgarp_mission }
					}
					else = { NOT = { has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_rumelia_mission } }
				}
			}
		}
		visible = { GER = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans } }
		on_map_mode = decision_view_only
		activation = { always = no }
		days_mission_timeout = 180
		highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { state = var:GER.ottoman_investment_targeted_state } }
		available = { hidden_trigger = { always = no } }
		is_good = yes
		timeout_effect = {

				limit = { GER = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_inGERstructure } }
				var:GER.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {

					add_building_construction = {
						type = inGERstructure
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				TUR_add_debt_5_GER = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { GER = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_consumer } }
				var:GER.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				TUR_add_debt_8_GER = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_military
							has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_dockyard
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { GER = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_military } }
					var:GER.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = arms_factory
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { GER = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_dockyard } }
					var:GER.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = dockyard
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
				TUR_add_debt_10_GER = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { GER = { has_idea = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
				GER = { remove_ideas = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { GER = { has_idea = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
				GER = { remove_ideas = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { GER = { has_idea = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
				GER = { remove_ideas = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans }
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = { GER = { has_idea = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
					GER = { remove_ideas = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { GER = { has_idea = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans } }

TUR_investing_in_the_sick_man = {
	invest_in_ottoman_rumelia = {
		icon = GFX_decision_hol_attract_foreign_investors
		allowed = { always = yes }
		target_trigger = { FROM = { tag = TUR } }
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = FROM
				has_country_flag = TUR_not_taking_investment_rumelia
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_tt
				NOT = {
					has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_rumelia_mission
					has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_anatolia_mission
					has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_syria_mission
					has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_mesapotamia_mission
					has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_trablusgarp_mission
				}
			}
		}
		cost = 50
		on_map_mode = decision_view_only
		fire_only_once = no
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_states_trigger = {
				is_controlled_by = TUR
				TUR_investment_state_rumelia = yes
			}
		}
		visible = {
			TUR = { any_owned_state = { TUR_investment_state_rumelia = yes } }
			NOT = {
				has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_rumelia_mission
				has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_anatolia_mission
				has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_syria_mission
				has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_mesapotamia_mission
				has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_trablusgarp_mission
				has_country_flag = TUR_not_taking_investment_at_all
				has_country_flag = TUR_not_taking_investment_rumelia
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			country_event = ottoman.40
			effect_tooltip = { activate_mission = invest_in_ottoman_rumelia_mission }
			set_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0.5
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories < 5
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories > 10
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories > 15
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories > 20
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories > 25
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories > 30
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = TUR
					value > 25
				}
				add = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = TUR
					value > 50
				}
				add = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = TUR
					value > 80
				}
				add = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction_with = TUR
				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war_together_with = TUR
				add = 15
			}
			modifier = {
				tag = RUS
				add = -10
			}
		}
	}

				limit = { has_idea = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans }
				remove_ideas = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans }
				remove_ideas = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans }
				remove_ideas = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans
			}
			clr_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans
			clr_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_infrastructure
			clr_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_consumer
			clr_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_military
			clr_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_dockyard
			clear_variable = var:ROOT.ottoman_investment_targeted_state
		}
	}
	invest_in_ottoman_anatolia = {
		icon = GFX_decision_hol_attract_foreign_investors
		allowed = { always = yes }
		target_trigger = { FROM = { tag = TUR } }
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = FROM
				has_country_flag = TUR_not_taking_investment_anatolia
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_tt
				NOT = {
					has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_rumelia_mission
					has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_anatolia_mission
					has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_syria_mission
					has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_mesapotamia_mission
					has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_trablusgarp_mission
				}
			}
		}
		cost = 50
		on_map_mode = decision_view_only
		fire_only_once = no
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_states_trigger = {
				is_controlled_by = TUR
				TUR_investment_state_anatolia = yes
			}
		}
		visible = {
			TUR = { any_owned_state = { TUR_investment_state_anatolia = yes } }
			NOT = {
				has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_rumelia_mission
				has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_anatolia_mission
				has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_syria_mission
				has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_mesapotamia_mission
				has_active_mission = invest_in_ottoman_trablusgarp_mission
				has_country_flag = TUR_not_taking_investment_at_all
				has_country_flag = TUR_not_taking_investment_anatolia
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			country_event = ottoman.41
			effect_tooltip = { activate_mission = invest_in_ottoman_anatolia_mission }
			set_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0.5
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories < 5
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories > 10
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories > 15
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories > 20
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories > 25
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories > 30
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = TUR
					value > 25
				}
				add = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = TUR
					value > 50
				}
				add = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = TUR
					value > 80
				}
				add = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction_with = TUR
				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war_together_with = TUR
				add = 15
			}
			modifier = {
				tag = RUS
				add = -10
			}
		}
	}
	invest_in_ottoman_anatolia_mission = {
		icon = GFX_decision_hol_attract_foreign_investors
		allowed = { always = yes }
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = TUR
				var:ROOT.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = { NOT = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = TUR } }
			}
		}
		activation = { always = no }
		days_mission_timeout = 180
		available = { hidden_trigger = { always = no } }

		highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { state = var:FRA.ottoman_investment_targeted_state } }

					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1

					}
				}

				}
				if = {
					limit = { tag = ENG }
					TUR = { TUR_add_debt_5_ENG = yes }
				}

				}

							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

			base = 0
			modifier = {
				date > 1914.1.10
				add = 1000
			}
		}
	}
